<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 8 – September 11</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>60 mph (95 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1004 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Gabrielle_(2007)" title="Tropical Storm Gabrielle (2007)">Tropical Storm Gabrielle (2007)</a></div>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Cold_front" title="Cold front">cold front</a> that moved off the southeastern coast of the United States on September 1 developed a weak low over the waters near <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a>. The low drifted eastward and weakened over the next few days until it joined with convection from an upper-level trough that had been moving over the western Atlantic.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gabrielletcr_42-0"><a href="#cite_note-gabrielletcr-42">[41]</a></sup> On September 8, the center of circulation became sufficiently organized to be declared Subtropical Storm Gabrielle, about 360 nautical miles (670 km) southeast of <a href="/wiki/Cape_Hatteras" title="Cape Hatteras">Cape Hatteras</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7LDisc1_43-0"><a href="#cite_note-7LDisc1-43">[42]</a></sup> For the next twelve hours, the system's strongest winds and thunderstorms remained separated from the center. On September 8 new convection eventually united with the center, leading the transition of Gabrielle into a tropical storm. Gabrielle gradually strengthened as it traveled northwest towards <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a> and <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">Virginia</a>. The storm reached its peak intensity of 60 mph (95 km/h) just before it arrived in <a href="/wiki/Cape_Lookout_(North_Carolina)" title="Cape Lookout (North Carolina)">Cape Lookout</a>, though strong wind shear kept most of the convection and surface winds offshore.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gabrielletcr_42-1"><a href="#cite_note-gabrielletcr-42">[41]</a></sup> Gabrielle weakened over land, and moved back into the Atlantic on September 10. The circulation deteriorated further, and the storm dissipated southwest of <a href="/wiki/Nova_Scotia" title="Nova Scotia">Nova Scotia</a> the next day.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7LDisc16_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-7LDisc16-44">[43]</a></sup></p>
<p>In advance of the storm, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_watches_and_warnings" title="Tropical cyclone watches and warnings">tropical cyclone watches and warnings</a> were issued for coastal areas,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gabrielletcr_42-2"><a href="#cite_note-gabrielletcr-42">[41]</a></sup> while rescue teams and the U.S. Coast Guard were put on standby.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USAtoday_45-0"><a href="#cite_note-USAtoday-45">[44]</a></sup> The storm dropped heavy rainfall near its immediate landfall location but little precipitation elsewhere. Along the coast, high waves, <a href="/wiki/Rip_current" title="Rip current">rip currents</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">storm surge</a> were reported. Slight localized flooding was reported. Gusty winds also occurred, though no wind damage was reported. Overall damage was minor, and there were no fatalities.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gabrielletcr_42-3"><a href="#cite_note-gabrielletcr-42">[41]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Ingrid">Tropical Storm Ingrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Ingrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg"><img alt="Ingrid 14 sept 2007 1310Z.jpg" data-file-height="1400" data-file-width="1400" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg/150px-Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg/225px-Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg/300px-Ingrid_14_sept_2007_1310Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ingrid_2007_track.png"><img alt="Ingrid 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Ingrid_2007_track.png/150px-Ingrid_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Ingrid_2007_track.png/225px-Ingrid_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Ingrid_2007_track.png/300px-Ingrid_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 12 – September 17</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>45 mph (75 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1002 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>A large tropical wave exited Africa on September 6 and initially failed to develop due to strong easterly shear. On September 9, a broad low pressure area developed about midway between Africa and the Lesser Antilles.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ingridtcr_46-0"><a href="#cite_note-ingridtcr-46">[45]</a></sup> The wind shear slowly weakened, and early on September 12 Tropical Depression Eight developed about 1125 miles (1815 km) east of the Lesser Antilles. The system moved west-northwestward due to a ridge to its north, and with continued wind shear, it remained a tropical depression for 24 hours before convection increased further. Early on September 13 it intensified into Tropical Storm Ingrid, reaching peak winds of 45 mph (75 km/h).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ingridtcr_46-1"><a href="#cite_note-ingridtcr-46">[45]</a></sup> Operationally, it was not upgraded to a tropical storm until that evening.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-td8adv7_47-0"><a href="#cite_note-td8adv7-47">[46]</a></sup></p>
<p>Ingrid remained a tropical storm until September 15, when it weakened to a tropical depression due to high shear from a strong <a href="/wiki/Tropical_upper_tropospheric_trough" title="Tropical upper tropospheric trough">tropical upper tropospheric trough</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ingridtcr_46-2"><a href="#cite_note-ingridtcr-46">[45]</a></sup> Gradual weakening continued as it passed northeast of the <a href="/wiki/Leeward_Islands" title="Leeward Islands">Leeward Islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-td8adv16_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-td8adv16-48">[47]</a></sup> Ingrid briefly reorganized on September 16,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49"><a href="#cite_note-49">[48]</a></sup> before weakening further and degenerating into an open wave early on September 17.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-td8adv20_50-0"><a href="#cite_note-td8adv20-50">[49]</a></sup> The remnants turned northwestward within the low-level steering flow, and dissipated on September 18 without redevelopment. There were no reports of damage or casualties associated with Ingrid because the storm never threatened land.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ingridtcr_46-3"><a href="#cite_note-ingridtcr-46">[45]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Humberto">Hurricane Humberto</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Hurricane Humberto">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">Category 1 hurricane (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg"><img alt="Humberto 12 sept 2007 2310Z.jpg" data-file-height="1400" data-file-width="1400" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg/150px-Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg/225px-Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg/300px-Humberto_12_sept_2007_2310Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Humberto_2007_track.png"><img alt="Humberto 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Humberto_2007_track.png/150px-Humberto_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Humberto_2007_track.png/225px-Humberto_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Humberto_2007_track.png/300px-Humberto_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 12 – September 14</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>90 mph (150 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  985 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Humberto_(2007)" title="Hurricane Humberto (2007)">Hurricane Humberto (2007)</a></div>
<p>On September 12, an area of thunderstorm activity in the Gulf of Mexico organized into Tropical Depression Nine, about 60 mi (97 km) southeast of <a href="/wiki/Matagorda,_Texas" title="Matagorda, Texas">Matagorda, Texas</a>. Within three hours of forming, it was named <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Humberto_(2007)" title="Hurricane Humberto (2007)">Tropical Storm Humberto</a>, and it turned to the north-northeast before rapidly intensifying.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-humbertotcr_51-0"><a href="#cite_note-humbertotcr-51">[50]</a></sup> In the early morning hours of September 13, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hunter" title="Hurricane Hunter">Hurricane Hunter</a> aircraft found that Humberto had strengthened into a hurricane while located about 15 miles (20 km) off the coast of Texas.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disc4_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-disc4-52">[51]</a></sup> Humberto quickly weakened and entered Southwest <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> as a tropical storm during the afternoon of September 13,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disc6_53-0"><a href="#cite_note-disc6-53">[52]</a></sup> dissipating the next day.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-humbertotcr_51-1"><a href="#cite_note-humbertotcr-51">[50]</a></sup></p>
<p>Hurricane Humberto caused some structural damage on <a href="/wiki/High_Island,_Texas" title="High Island, Texas">High Island</a> and widespread tree and power line damage in the <a href="/wiki/Beaumont,_Texas" title="Beaumont, Texas">Beaumont</a>-<a href="/wiki/Port_Arthur,_Texas" title="Port Arthur, Texas">Port Arthur</a> area.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Enterprise_.E2.80.93_Hurricane_Humberto_hammers_SE_Texas_54-0"><a href="#cite_note-Enterprise_.E2.80.93_Hurricane_Humberto_hammers_SE_Texas-54">[53]</a></sup> Power outages caused four <a href="/wiki/Oil_refinery" title="Oil refinery">oil refineries</a> to halt production in <a href="/wiki/Beaumont,_Texas" title="Beaumont, Texas">Beaumont</a>. One person was reported dead as a result of the storm, a <a href="/wiki/Bridge_City,_Texas" title="Bridge City, Texas">Bridge City</a> man killed when his carport crashed on him outside his house. Damage was estimated at $50 million.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Enterprise_.E2.80.93_Hurricane_Humberto_hammers_SE_Texas_54-1"><a href="#cite_note-Enterprise_.E2.80.93_Hurricane_Humberto_hammers_SE_Texas-54">[53]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Ten">Tropical Depression Ten</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression Ten">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg"><img alt="TD Ten 21 sept 2007 1650Z.jpg" data-file-height="4800" data-file-width="4200" height="171" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg/150px-TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg/225px-TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg/300px-TD_Ten_21_sept_2007_1650Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:10-L_2007_track.png"><img alt="10-L 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/10-L_2007_track.png/150px-10-L_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/10-L_2007_track.png/225px-10-L_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/10-L_2007_track.png/300px-10-L_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 21 – September 22</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>35 mph (55 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1005 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Depression_Ten_(2007)" title="Tropical Depression Ten (2007)">Tropical Depression Ten (2007)</a></div>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Subtropical_cyclone" title="Subtropical cyclone">subtropical depression</a> formed on September 21 in the northeastern <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a> from the interaction of a <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">tropical wave</a>, the tail end of a <a href="/wiki/Cold_front" title="Cold front">cold front</a>, and an upper-level <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">low</a>. Initially containing a poorly defined circulation and intermittent thunderstorm activity, the system transitioned into a tropical depression after <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_convection" title="Atmospheric convection">convection</a> increased over the center. Tracking northwestward, the depression moved ashore near <a href="/wiki/Fort_Walton_Beach,_Florida" title="Fort Walton Beach, Florida">Fort Walton Beach</a> early on September 22, and shortly thereafter it <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone#Dissipation" title="Tropical cyclone">dissipated</a> over southeastern <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TenTCR_55-0"><a href="#cite_note-TenTCR-55">[54]</a></sup></p>
<p>It was the first tropical cyclone to threaten the New Orleans area after the destructive <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">2005 hurricane season</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">Hurricane Katrina</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56"><a href="#cite_note-56">[55]</a></sup> Overall impact from the cyclone was minor and largely limited to light rainfall.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-hpc4a_57-0"><a href="#cite_note-hpc4a-57">[56]</a></sup> However, the precursor system spawned a damaging tornado in <a href="/wiki/Eustis,_Florida" title="Eustis, Florida">Eustis, Florida</a>, where 20 houses were destroyed and 30 more were damaged.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[57]</a></sup> Damage was estimated at $6.2 million.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TenTCR_55-1"><a href="#cite_note-TenTCR-55">[54]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Jerry">Tropical Storm Jerry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Jerry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg"><img alt="Jerry 24 sept 2007 1259Z.jpg" data-file-height="1400" data-file-width="1400" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg/150px-Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg/225px-Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg/300px-Jerry_24_sept_2007_1259Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jerry_2007_track.png"><img alt="Jerry 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Jerry_2007_track.png/150px-Jerry_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Jerry_2007_track.png/225px-Jerry_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Jerry_2007_track.png/300px-Jerry_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 23 – September 24</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>40 mph (65 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1003 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>The origins of Jerry were from a non-tropical <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">low pressure area</a> over the central Atlantic on September 21. The system meandered for two days, gradually developing deeper convection and gaining organization. On September 23, the <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">National Hurricane Center</a> declared it a subtropical depression, as a warm <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">core</a> had developed but the system was still involved with an upper-level low, and its strongest winds were well removed from the center.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jerrytcr_59-0"><a href="#cite_note-jerrytcr-59">[58]</a></sup> Early on September 23, both <a href="/wiki/Satellite" title="Satellite">satellite</a> estimates and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/QuikScat" title="QuikScat">QuikScat</a> data determined that the depression had strengthened into Subtropical Storm Jerry, despite the lack of a well-defined inner core.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11LDisc2_60-0"><a href="#cite_note-11LDisc2-60">[59]</a></sup></p>
<p>The storm slowly acquired tropical characteristics including a better-defined warm core,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11LDisc3_61-0"><a href="#cite_note-11LDisc3-61">[60]</a></sup> and Jerry became fully tropical that evening as a weak and <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">sheared</a> tropical storm with 40 mph (65 km/h) winds over a small radius.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jerrytcr_59-1"><a href="#cite_note-jerrytcr-59">[58]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11LDisc4_62-0"><a href="#cite_note-11LDisc4-62">[61]</a></sup> It accelerated northeastward over cooler waters with <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">sea surface temperatures</a> below 75 °F (24 °C).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11LDisc5_63-0"><a href="#cite_note-11LDisc5-63">[62]</a></sup> On September 24, it weakened to a tropical depression ahead of a powerful <a href="/wiki/Cold_front" title="Cold front">cold front</a> with little deep convection remaining in the system.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11LDisc6_64-0"><a href="#cite_note-11LDisc6-64">[63]</a></sup> That evening, a QuikScat pass determined that Jerry opened up into a <a href="/wiki/Trough_(meteorology)" title="Trough (meteorology)">trough</a>, which was being absorbed into the larger <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frontal_system" title="Frontal system">frontal system</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11LDisc8_65-0"><a href="#cite_note-11LDisc8-65">[64]</a></sup> It completely dissipated by early on September 25. Jerry never approached land during its lifespan, and no damage or casualties were reported.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-jerrytcr_59-2"><a href="#cite_note-jerrytcr-59">[58]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Karen">Hurricane Karen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Hurricane Karen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">Category 1 hurricane (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg"><img alt="Karen 26 sept 2007 1220Z.jpg" data-file-height="1800" data-file-width="1800" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg/150px-Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg/225px-Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg/300px-Karen_26_sept_2007_1220Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Karen_2007_track.png"><img alt="Karen 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Karen_2007_track.png/150px-Karen_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Karen_2007_track.png/225px-Karen_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Karen_2007_track.png/300px-Karen_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 25 – September 29</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>75 mph (120 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  988 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Karen_(2007)" title="Hurricane Karen (2007)">Hurricane Karen (2007)</a></div>
<p>A very large tropical wave accompanied by a large envelope of low pressure emerged from the coast of <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a> on September 21. As it moved westward, deep convection gradually increased over the disturbance as its broad low-level circulation became better-defined. By September 24, as the system traveled northwestward it organized enough to become a tropical depression.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-karentcr_66-0"><a href="#cite_note-karentcr-66">[65]</a></sup> Six hours later the depression was upgraded to Tropical Storm Karen.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12LDisc2_67-0"><a href="#cite_note-12LDisc2-67">[66]</a></sup></p>
<p>Karen's organization and intensity remained steady for the next day. Early on September 26, however, the storm strengthened significantly. In post-operational analysis the cyclone was determined to have reached hurricane-strength for about twelve hours.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-karentcr_66-1"><a href="#cite_note-karentcr-66">[65]</a></sup> The strengthening was short-lived because a sharp upper-level trough to the west of Karen increased the amount of vertical <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">wind shear</a> over the hurricane. By September 28 these unfavorable conditions had weakened Karen to a marginal tropical storm and left its low-level circulation exposed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12LDisc14_68-0"><a href="#cite_note-12LDisc14-68">[67]</a></sup> Meanwhile, the storm began heading northward and experiencing intermittent bursts of deep convection. However, the relentless wind shear exposed the system's circulation until it dissipated in the mid-Atlantic on September 29. Karen's remnants lingered near the <a href="/wiki/Leeward_Islands" title="Leeward Islands">Leeward Islands</a> for the next few days, although the system never directly affected land. As a result, no reported damages or casualties were associated with Karen.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-karentcr_66-2"><a href="#cite_note-karentcr-66">[65]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Lorenzo">Hurricane Lorenzo</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Hurricane Lorenzo">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">Category 1 hurricane (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg"><img alt="Lorenzo 27 sept 2007 1920Z.jpg" data-file-height="3600" data-file-width="4000" height="135" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg/150px-Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg/225px-Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg/300px-Lorenzo_27_sept_2007_1920Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lorenzo_2007_track.png"><img alt="Lorenzo 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Lorenzo_2007_track.png/150px-Lorenzo_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Lorenzo_2007_track.png/225px-Lorenzo_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Lorenzo_2007_track.png/300px-Lorenzo_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 25 – September 28</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>80 mph (130 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  990 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Lorenzo" title="Hurricane Lorenzo">Hurricane Lorenzo</a></div>
<p>A <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">tropical wave</a> moved off the western coast of <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a> on September 11,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lorenzotcr_69-0"><a href="#cite_note-lorenzotcr-69">[68]</a></sup> traversed the Caribbean and crossed the Yucatán on September 21. The disturbance developed a small surface <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">low</a> on September 24 while moving erratically over the southwestern Gulf of Mexico.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lorenzotcr_69-1"><a href="#cite_note-lorenzotcr-69">[68]</a></sup> Strong <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">upper-level winds</a> initially prevented the system from developing convection; however, the shear relaxed on the following day and convection increased.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lorenzotcr_69-2"><a href="#cite_note-lorenzotcr-69">[68]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sept_24_530pm_TWO_70-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sept_24_530pm_TWO-70">[69]</a></sup> On the evening of September 25, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hunters" title="Hurricane Hunters">Hurricane Hunter</a> aircraft found evidence that the low qualified as a tropical depression.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13L_Disc_1_71-0"><a href="#cite_note-13L_Disc_1-71">[70]</a></sup> Under weak steering currents, the depression drifted south and southwest, executing a small cyclonic loop into the <a href="/wiki/Bay_of_Campeche" title="Bay of Campeche">Bay of Campeche</a>. Upper-level winds gave way to an anticyclone above the depression, and the system became Tropical Storm Lorenzo on September 27 about 130 nautical miles (240 km) east of <a href="/wiki/Tuxpan" title="Tuxpan">Tuxpan</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lorenzotcr_69-3"><a href="#cite_note-lorenzotcr-69">[68]</a></sup> Rapid intensification brought Lorenzo to hurricane status early that evening, less than twelve hours after becoming a tropical storm. Lorenzo reached its peak intensity on September 28, then weakened slightly before making landfall near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tecolutla,_Mexico" title="Tecolutla, Mexico">Tecolutla, Mexico</a> as a minimal hurricane. The small circulation weakened rapidly after landfall, and the system dissipated the next day.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lorenzotcr_69-4"><a href="#cite_note-lorenzotcr-69">[68]</a></sup></p>
<p>Six deaths in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a> were attributed to Lorenzo, mostly due to flash floods and mudslides. The states of <a href="/wiki/Puebla" title="Puebla">Puebla</a> and <a href="/wiki/Veracruz" title="Veracruz">Veracruz</a> reported damage from rain and high winds. Two hundred people were forced to evacuate in <a href="/wiki/Hidalgo_(state)" title="Hidalgo (state)">Hidalgo</a> when the <a href="/wiki/San_Lorenzo_River_(Mexico)" title="San Lorenzo River (Mexico)">San Lorenzo River</a> overflowed its banks. Lorenzo made landfall in virtually the same location that Hurricane Dean had struck a month earlier.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lorenzotcr_69-5"><a href="#cite_note-lorenzotcr-69">[68]</a></sup> Damage was estimated at $1 billion (2007 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MXN" title="MXN">MXN</a>; $92 million 2007 USD, $106 million 2017 USD).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72"><a href="#cite_note-72">[71]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Melissa">Tropical Storm Melissa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Melissa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg"><img alt="Melissa 29 sept 2007 1245Z.jpg" data-file-height="4000" data-file-width="3600" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg/150px-Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg/225px-Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/79/Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg/300px-Melissa_29_sept_2007_1245Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Melissa_2007_track.png"><img alt="Melissa 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Melissa_2007_track.png/150px-Melissa_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Melissa_2007_track.png/225px-Melissa_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Melissa_2007_track.png/300px-Melissa_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>September 28 – September 30</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>40 mph (65 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1005 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>On September 26, a tropical wave exited Africa and quickly developed a low pressure area. Following a convective increase and better-defined outflow, it developed into Tropical Depression Fourteen about 115 miles (185 km) west-southwest of the southernmost Cape Verde Islands early on September 28.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-melissatcr_73-0"><a href="#cite_note-melissatcr-73">[72]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14LDisc1_74-0"><a href="#cite_note-14LDisc1-74">[73]</a></sup> Because the depression was isolated from the <a href="/wiki/Subtropical_ridge" title="Subtropical ridge">subtropical ridge</a>, the depression drifted west-northwestward.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-melissatcr_73-1"><a href="#cite_note-melissatcr-73">[72]</a></sup> Westerly wind shear prevented significant development,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14LDisc3_75-0"><a href="#cite_note-14LDisc3-75">[74]</a></sup> but following an increase in convection, the depression intensified into Tropical Storm Melissa early on September 29.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14LDisc4_76-0"><a href="#cite_note-14LDisc4-76">[75]</a></sup> Similar to previous storms Ingrid and <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Karen_(2007)" title="Hurricane Karen (2007)">Karen</a>, high wind shear in the deep tropics hindered Melissa's development,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14LDisc5_77-0"><a href="#cite_note-14LDisc5-77">[76]</a></sup> and its peak winds were only 40 mph (65 km/h);<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-melissatcr_73-2"><a href="#cite_note-melissatcr-73">[72]</a></sup> operationally, satellite imagery suggested the storm reached 45 mph (72 km/h).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14LDisc7_78-0"><a href="#cite_note-14LDisc7-78">[77]</a></sup> By September 30, the shear and cooler waters weakened Melissa to a tropical depression with a poorly defined surface center.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14LDisc9_79-0"><a href="#cite_note-14LDisc9-79">[78]</a></sup> The system lost its deep convection and by that afternoon, Melissa degenerated into a remnant low.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[79]</a></sup> It continued west-northwestward, producing intermittent convection, until being absorbed by a front northeast of the <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">Lesser Antilles</a> on October 5. There were no reports of damage or casualties.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-melissatcr_73-3"><a href="#cite_note-melissatcr-73">[72]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Depression_Fifteen">Tropical Depression Fifteen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Tropical Depression Fifteen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #5ebaff">Tropical depression (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg"><img alt="TD 15 11 oct 2007 1321Z.jpg" data-file-height="1400" data-file-width="1400" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg/150px-TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg/225px-TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg/300px-TD_15_11_oct_2007_1321Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:15-L_2007_track.png"><img alt="15-L 2007 track.png" data-file-height="664" data-file-width="1024" height="97" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/15-L_2007_track.png/150px-15-L_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/15-L_2007_track.png/225px-15-L_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/15-L_2007_track.png/300px-15-L_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>October 11 – October 12</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>35 mph (55 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1011 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>An area of disturbed weather extended from the northwestern <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">Caribbean Sea</a> to the western <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic Ocean</a> on October 4,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15TCR_81-0"><a href="#cite_note-15TCR-81">[80]</a></sup> possibly related to the remnants of <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Karen_(2007)" title="Hurricane Karen (2007)">Hurricane Karen</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D1_82-0"><a href="#cite_note-D1-82">[81]</a></sup> The system slowly organized, developing a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Low_pressure_area" title="Low pressure area">surface low pressure</a> on October 8 to the northeast of the <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">Turks and Caicos Islands</a>. <a href="/wiki/Atmospheric_convection" title="Atmospheric convection">Convection</a> associated with the storm steadily increased as the low moved towards the northeast.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15TCR_81-1"><a href="#cite_note-15TCR-81">[80]</a></sup> By October 11, the low organized into Tropical Depression Fifteen about 740 mi (1,190 km) east-southeast of <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PA1_83-0"><a href="#cite_note-PA1-83">[82]</a></sup> after the convection had persisted for about 12 hours. An upper-level low to the west caused strong southwesterly wind shear, which inhibited development.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D1_82-1"><a href="#cite_note-D1-82">[81]</a></sup></p>
<p>On October 12, a building ridge caused the depression to slow at the same time as the convection began decreasing.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D3_84-0"><a href="#cite_note-D3-84">[83]</a></sup> The storm's center became exposed as the deep convection became limited to a few small cells north of the center.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D4_85-0"><a href="#cite_note-D4-85">[84]</a></sup> By that afternoon, the depression degenerated into a remnant low.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-D5_86-0"><a href="#cite_note-D5-86">[85]</a></sup> The remnant low persisted for the next several days while picking up speed and taking a gradual turn towards the northeast. The low transitioned into an <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">extratropical cyclone</a> on October 14 and intensified, moving through the <a href="/wiki/Azores" title="Azores">Azores</a> with gale-force winds. It reached winds of 50 mph (85 km/h) before being absorbed by a larger extratropical storm on October 18.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15TCR_81-2"><a href="#cite_note-15TCR-81">[80]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Noel">Hurricane Noel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Hurricane Noel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">Category 1 hurricane (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg"><img alt="Noel 01 nov 2007 1815Z.jpg" data-file-height="7200" data-file-width="5600" height="193" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg/150px-Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg/225px-Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg/300px-Noel_01_nov_2007_1815Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Noel_2007_track.png"><img alt="Noel 2007 track.png" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="1024" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Noel_2007_track.png/150px-Noel_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Noel_2007_track.png/225px-Noel_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b5/Noel_2007_track.png/300px-Noel_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>October 28 – November 2</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>80 mph (130 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  980 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Noel" title="Hurricane Noel">Hurricane Noel</a></div>
<p>During the evening of October 27 a low pressure system that had been slowly developing over the eastern Caribbean organization into Tropical Depression Sixteen. The next day, it was upgraded to <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Noel" title="Hurricane Noel">Tropical Storm Noel</a> and made landfall on Haiti on October 29. Noel meandered across the western Caribbean for the next three days; the storm intensified into a hurricane on November 1. Tracking northward, it began its transition into an <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">extratropical cyclone</a> on November 2, becoming fully extratropical on November 4 while over <a href="/wiki/Labrador" title="Labrador">Labrador</a>. As a powerful <a href="/wiki/Extratropical_cyclone" title="Extratropical cyclone">extratropical cyclone</a>, it crossed back into the Atlantic and began a track towards western <a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Noel_TCR_87-0"><a href="#cite_note-Noel_TCR-87">[86]</a></sup></p>
<p>Throughout the Caribbean, Hurricane Noel caused severe damage. Torrential rainfall and mudslides caused by the storm killed at least 87 people in the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">Dominican Republic</a> and at least 73 in <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Noel_TCR_87-1"><a href="#cite_note-Noel_TCR-87">[86]</a></sup> Noel generated winds of 130 mph (210 km/h) in the <a href="/wiki/Wreckhouse,_Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Wreckhouse, Newfoundland and Labrador">Wreckhouse</a> region of <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Newfoundland and Labrador">Newfoundland and Labrador</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CTV_88-0"><a href="#cite_note-CTV-88">[87]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Olga">Tropical Storm Olga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Olga">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">Tropical storm (SSHWS)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
<div style="vertical-align: middle"><span class="nowrap"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Olga2007.jpg"><img alt="Olga2007.jpg" data-file-height="924" data-file-width="1050" height="132" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Olga2007.jpg/150px-Olga2007.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Olga2007.jpg/225px-Olga2007.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/ba/Olga2007.jpg/300px-Olga2007.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a><span class="nowrap"> </span><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Olga_2007_track.png"><img alt="Olga 2007 track.png" data-file-height="633" data-file-width="1024" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Olga_2007_track.png/150px-Olga_2007_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Olga_2007_track.png/225px-Olga_2007_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Olga_2007_track.png/300px-Olga_2007_track.png 2x" width="150"/></a></span></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Duration</th>
<td>December 11 – December 13</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row">Peak intensity</th>
<td>60 mph (95 km/h) <small>(1-min)</small>  1003 <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">mbar</a> (<a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">hPa</a>)</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Olga_(2007)" title="Tropical Storm Olga (2007)">Tropical Storm Olga (2007)</a></div>
<p>In the second week of December, after the official end of the hurricane season, a low developed east of the northernmost <a href="/wiki/Lesser_Antilles" title="Lesser Antilles">Lesser Antilles</a>. It slowly acquired tropical characteristics, and late on December 10, the National Hurricane Center declared it Subtropical Storm Olga while just north of <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>. It is the first post-season storm since <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Zeta_(2005)" title="Tropical Storm Zeta (2005)">Tropical Storm Zeta</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">2005 season</a>. Olga was only one of a few out of season tropical cyclones to make landfall. The storm made landfall on December 11 on the eastern tip of the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">Dominican Republic</a>. Later that evening, Olga transitioned into a tropical storm just after making landfall. Olga tracked over <a href="/wiki/Hispaniola" title="Hispaniola">Hispaniola</a> and emerged in the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">Caribbean Sea</a>. Strong <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">wind shear</a> and dry air caused Olga to weaken into a remnant low early on December 13.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OlgaTCR_89-0"><a href="#cite_note-OlgaTCR-89">[88]</a></sup></p>
<p>The storm impacted many areas affected by <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Noel" title="Hurricane Noel">Tropical Storm Noel</a> a month earlier. In Puerto Rico, moderate rainfall caused one death. According to the National Hurricane Center's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Cyclone_Report" title="Tropical Cyclone Report">Tropical Cyclone Report</a> on Olga, at least 22 occurred due to the release of floodgates at a dam in <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Province_(Dominican_Republic)" title="Santiago Province (Dominican Republic)">Santiago Province</a>. Two deaths were also reported in <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>, and one fatality was confirmed in <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>. Almost 12,000 homes were damaged, of which 370 were completely destroyed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-OlgaTCR_89-1"><a href="#cite_note-OlgaTCR-89">[88]</a></sup></p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Storm_names">Storm names</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Storm names">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The names to the right were used for storms that formed in the Atlantic basin in 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90"><a href="#cite_note-90">[89]</a></sup> This is the same list used in the <a href="/wiki/2001_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2001 Atlantic hurricane season">2001 season</a> except for Andrea, Ingrid, and Melissa, which replaced <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Allison" title="Tropical Storm Allison">Allison</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Iris" title="Hurricane Iris">Iris</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Michelle" title="Hurricane Michelle">Michelle</a>, respectively and were first used in 2007. Names that were not assigned are marked in <span style="color:#666666">gray</span>.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Retirement">Retirement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Retirement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On May 13, 2008, at the 30th Session of the <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">World Meteorological Organization</a>'s Regional Association IV Hurricane Committee, the WMO retired the names <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dean_(2007)" title="Hurricane Dean (2007)">Dean</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Felix_(2007)" title="Hurricane Felix (2007)">Felix</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Noel_(2007)" title="Hurricane Noel (2007)">Noel</a> from its <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lists_of_tropical_cyclone_names#North_Atlantic" title="Lists of tropical cyclone names">rotating name lists</a>. The names were replaced with <i>Dorian</i>, <i>Fernand</i>, and <i>Nestor</i> for the <a href="/wiki/2013_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2013 Atlantic hurricane season">2013 season</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91"><a href="#cite_note-91">[90]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_effects">Season effects</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Season effects">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>This is a table of the storms in the 2007 Atlantic hurricane season. It mentions all of the season's storms and their names, landfall(s), peak intensities, damages, and death totals. Deaths in parentheses are additional and indirect (an example of such being a traffic accident or landslide), but are still related to that storm. The damage and death totals in this list include impacts when the storm was a precursor wave or post-tropical low, and all of the damage figures are in 2007 USD.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2007_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="mw-references-wrap">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The cumulative damage figures were obtained by summing the damage figures on the individual Tropical Cyclone Reports referenced throughout the article, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dean" title="Hurricane Dean">Hurricane Dean</a>. Dean's damage figures were obtained by adding the per-country totals referenced in the <a href="#Impact">Impact</a> section of this article.</span></li>
</ol>
